<tr style="border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px; vertical-align: top; background-color: #F7F7F7"><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px; white-space: nowrap; background-image: url(tbl_bck110.png)" id="item.EmCare.C10.IT.DE01" class="hierarchy"><img src="tbl_spacer.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vline.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vjoin.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="icon-q-display.png" alt="." style="background-color: #F7F7F7; background-color: inherit" title="Display" class="hierarchy"/> EmCare.C10.IT.DE01</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">&lt;h1&gt;Very Severe Disease&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;Give one dose of rectal diazepam if convulsing now, repeat after 10 minutes if convulsion has not stopped&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;Give any pre-referral treatment immediately&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;Treat to prevent low blood sugar&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;Keep the child warm&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;Refer &lt;span class=&quot;caps&quot;&gt;URGENTLY&lt;/span&gt; to hospital*.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;*Exception: If lethargy is the only sign and child is dehydrated, rehydrated and assess.&lt;/p&gt;</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">0..1</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/R4/codesystem-item-type.html#item-type-display">display</a></td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"/><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">Expressions: <ul><li style="font-size: 11px"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/uv/sdc/StructureDefinition/sdc-questionnaire-enableWhenExpression">Enable When</a>: <code>%resource.repeat(item).where(linkId='load-EmCare.C10.IT.DE01').answer.first().value=true</code></li></ul></td></tr>
<tr style="border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px; vertical-align: top; background-color: white"><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px; white-space: nowrap; background-image: url(tbl_bck110.png)" id="item.EmCare.C10.IT.DE02" class="hierarchy"><img src="tbl_spacer.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vline.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vjoin.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="icon-q-display.png" alt="." style="background-color: white; background-color: inherit" title="Display" class="hierarchy"/> EmCare.C10.IT.DE02</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">&lt;h1&gt;Severe Pneumonia or Very Severe Disease&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;Give first dose of intramuscular Cefotaxime&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢If wheezing present, give one dose of rapid acting bronchodilator* pre-referral&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Treat the child to prevent low blood sugar&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Refer &lt;span class=&quot;caps&quot;&gt;URGENTLY&lt;/span&gt; to hospital&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;*Nebulized salbutamol, salbutamol inhaler with spacer, or subcutaneous epinephrine (adrenaline)&lt;/p&gt;</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">0..1</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/R4/codesystem-item-type.html#item-type-display">display</a></td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"/><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">Expressions: <ul><li style="font-size: 11px"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/uv/sdc/StructureDefinition/sdc-questionnaire-enableWhenExpression">Enable When</a>: <code>%resource.repeat(item).where(linkId='load-EmCare.C10.IT.DE02').answer.first().value=true</code></li></ul></td></tr>
<tr style="border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px; vertical-align: top; background-color: #F7F7F7"><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px; white-space: nowrap; background-image: url(tbl_bck110.png)" id="item.EmCare.C10.IT.DE03" class="hierarchy"><img src="tbl_spacer.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vline.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vjoin.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="icon-q-display.png" alt="." style="background-color: #F7F7F7; background-color: inherit" title="Display" class="hierarchy"/> EmCare.C10.IT.DE03</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">&lt;h1&gt;Pneumonia&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢**Give oral Amoxicillin twice daily for 5 days**&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢If wheezing (or disappeared after inhaled salbutamol) give inhaled or oral salbutamol three times a day for 5 days*&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Soothe the throat and relieve the cough with a safe remedy.&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢If coughing for ≥14 days or recurrent wheeze, refer for possible TB or asthma assessment&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Advise mother when to return immediately&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Follow-up in 3 days&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Give oral Zinc once daily for 10-14 days.&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;*If inhaled bronchodilator is not available, oral salbutamol may be tried but not recommended for treatment of severe acute wheeze.&lt;/p&gt;</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">0..1</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/R4/codesystem-item-type.html#item-type-display">display</a></td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"/><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">Expressions: <ul><li style="font-size: 11px"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/uv/sdc/StructureDefinition/sdc-questionnaire-enableWhenExpression">Enable When</a>: <code>%resource.repeat(item).where(linkId='load-EmCare.C10.IT.DE03').answer.first().value=true</code></li></ul></td></tr>
<tr style="border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px; vertical-align: top; background-color: white"><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px; white-space: nowrap; background-image: url(tbl_bck110.png)" id="item.EmCare.C10.IT.DE04" class="hierarchy"><img src="tbl_spacer.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vline.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vjoin.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="icon-q-display.png" alt="." style="background-color: white; background-color: inherit" title="Display" class="hierarchy"/> EmCare.C10.IT.DE04</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">&lt;h1&gt;Cough or Cold&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢If wheezing (or disappeared after inhaled salbutamol) give inhaled or oral salbutamol three times a day for 5 days**&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Soothe the throat and relieve the cough with a safe remedy.&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢If coughing for ≥14 days or recurrent wheeze, refer for possible TB or asthma assessment&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Advise mother when to return immediately&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Follow-up in 5 days if not improving&lt;/p&gt;</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">0..1</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/R4/codesystem-item-type.html#item-type-display">display</a></td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"/><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">Expressions: <ul><li style="font-size: 11px"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/uv/sdc/StructureDefinition/sdc-questionnaire-enableWhenExpression">Enable When</a>: <code>%resource.repeat(item).where(linkId='load-EmCare.C10.IT.DE04').answer.first().value=true</code></li></ul></td></tr>
<tr style="border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px; vertical-align: top; background-color: #F7F7F7"><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px; white-space: nowrap; background-image: url(tbl_bck110.png)" id="item.EmCare.C10.IT.DE05" class="hierarchy"><img src="tbl_spacer.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vline.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vjoin.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="icon-q-display.png" alt="." style="background-color: #F7F7F7; background-color: inherit" title="Display" class="hierarchy"/> EmCare.C10.IT.DE05</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">&lt;h1&gt;Severe Dehydration&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ If child has no other severe classification:* Give fluid for severe dehydration (plan C) OR&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;If child also has another severe classification:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

    * &lt;b&gt;Refer &lt;span class=&quot;caps&quot;&gt;URGENTLY&lt;/span&gt; to hospital with mother giving frequent sips of &lt;span class=&quot;caps&quot;&gt;ORS&lt;/span&gt; on the way.&lt;/b&gt;
    * &lt;b&gt;Advise the mother to continue breastfeeding.&lt;/b&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢If child is 2 years or older and there is cholera in your area, give oral co-trimoxazole twice daily for 3 days or oral erythromycin 4 times a day for 3 days for cholera.&lt;/p&gt;</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">0..1</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/R4/codesystem-item-type.html#item-type-display">display</a></td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"/><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">Expressions: <ul><li style="font-size: 11px"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/uv/sdc/StructureDefinition/sdc-questionnaire-enableWhenExpression">Enable When</a>: <code>%resource.repeat(item).where(linkId='load-EmCare.C10.IT.DE05').answer.first().value=true</code></li></ul></td></tr>
<tr style="border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px; vertical-align: top; background-color: white"><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px; white-space: nowrap; background-image: url(tbl_bck110.png)" id="item.EmCare.C10.IT.DE06" class="hierarchy"><img src="tbl_spacer.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vline.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vjoin.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="icon-q-display.png" alt="." style="background-color: white; background-color: inherit" title="Display" class="hierarchy"/> EmCare.C10.IT.DE06</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">&lt;h1&gt;Some Dehydration&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Give Plan B for some dehydration:&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Give &lt;span class=&quot;caps&quot;&gt;ORS&lt;/span&gt; over 4 hrs in clinic, reassess for dehydration and select appropriate plan to continue treatment&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;If mother must leave before completing treatment, give &lt;span class=&quot;caps&quot;&gt;ORS&lt;/span&gt; for 4 hr Plan B treatment plus 2 packets as recommended in Plan A&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;At home, give extra fluid (as much as the child will take)&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Give oral Zinc once daily for 10 &amp;#8211; 14 days&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Continue feeding (exclusive breastfeeding if under 6 months)&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;If child also has another severe classification:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

		&lt;li&gt;&lt;b&gt;Advise the mother to continue breastfeeding.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Advise mother when to return immediately.&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Follow-up in 5 days if not improving.&lt;/p&gt;</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">0..1</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/R4/codesystem-item-type.html#item-type-display">display</a></td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"/><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">Expressions: <ul><li style="font-size: 11px"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/uv/sdc/StructureDefinition/sdc-questionnaire-enableWhenExpression">Enable When</a>: <code>%resource.repeat(item).where(linkId='load-EmCare.C10.IT.DE06').answer.first().value=true</code></li></ul></td></tr>

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;Give single dose of intramuscular benzathine penicillin, or if unavailable give oral amoxicillin twice daily for 10 days; if allergic to penicillin give oral erythromycin 4 times daily for 10 days&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ **Give oral paracetamol for pain or high fever (38.5°C or above), continue to give every 6 hours (4 times / day) until pain and/or high fever gone. **&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ Soothe the throat with a safe remedy.&lt;/p&gt;

<tr style="border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px; vertical-align: top; background-color: #F7F7F7"><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px; white-space: nowrap; background-image: url(tbl_bck110.png)" id="item.EmCare.C10.IT.DE28" class="hierarchy"><img src="tbl_spacer.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vline.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vjoin.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="icon-q-display.png" alt="." style="background-color: #F7F7F7; background-color: inherit" title="Display" class="hierarchy"/> EmCare.C10.IT.DE28</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">&lt;h1&gt;Papular Urticaria or Papular Pruritic Eruptions&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Trim finger nails and avoid scratching.&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Apply 1% hydrocortisone to new, inflamed lesions for five days.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Give oral antihistamine to relieve itch:
		&lt;ul&gt;
			&lt;li&gt;Short term use: Chlorphenamine, oral, 0.1mg/kg/ dose 6-8 hourly&lt;/li&gt;
			&lt;li&gt;Long term use for children 2-6 years: Cetirizine,oral, 5mg once daily&lt;/li&gt;
			&lt;li&gt;Caution: Do not give antihistamines to children&lt; 2 years of age.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Refer if no improvement after 2 weeks or if underlying malignancy or systemic disease is suspected.&lt;/p&gt;</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">0..1</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/R4/codesystem-item-type.html#item-type-display">display</a></td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"/><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">Expressions: <ul><li style="font-size: 11px"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/uv/sdc/StructureDefinition/sdc-questionnaire-enableWhenExpression">Enable When</a>: <code>%resource.repeat(item).where(linkId='load-EmCare.C10.IT.DE28').answer.first().value=true</code></li></ul></td></tr>

	&lt;p&gt;➢Avoid sharing clothes, towels and toiletries (e.g. brushes and combs) to prevent spreading the infection to others.&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Wash and dry skin well before applying treatment.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Apply an imidazole (e.g. clotrimazole 1% cream) three times daily until two weeks after lesions have cleared.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;For scalp infections (tinea capitis) give oral fluconazole 6mg/kg once daily for 28 days&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">0..1</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/R4/codesystem-item-type.html#item-type-display">display</a></td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"/><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">Expressions: <ul><li style="font-size: 11px"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/uv/sdc/StructureDefinition/sdc-questionnaire-enableWhenExpression">Enable When</a>: <code>%resource.repeat(item).where(linkId='load-EmCare.C10.IT.DE29').answer.first().value=true</code></li></ul></td></tr>

	&lt;p&gt;➢All close contacts should be treated simultaneously (even if not itchy).&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Wash all bed linen and underwear in hot water&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Expose all bedding to direct sunlight.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Put on clean clothes after treatment.
 &lt;br /&gt;
➢Treat the child and contacts under 6 years of age with Permethrin:&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Apply permethrin 5% lotion. Leave on overnight and washoff in the morning (may be repeated after one week).&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Treatment may need to be repeated after one week.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Treat secondary bacterial infection, if present, with Oral Cephalexin 12-25mg/kg/dose 6 hourly for 5 days&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Treat contacts over 6 years of age with Benzyl Benzoate:&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Apply benzyl benzoate 25% from the neck to the toes. Allow the lotion to remain on the body for 24 hours, then wash off using soap and water&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Treatment may need to be repeated after one week.&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">0..1</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/R4/codesystem-item-type.html#item-type-display">display</a></td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"/><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">Expressions: <ul><li style="font-size: 11px"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/uv/sdc/StructureDefinition/sdc-questionnaire-enableWhenExpression">Enable When</a>: <code>%resource.repeat(item).where(linkId='load-EmCare.C10.IT.DE30').answer.first().value=true</code></li></ul></td></tr>

	&lt;p&gt;➢Limit contact with other children and pregnant women until all lesions have crusted.&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Ensure adequate hydration.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Cut fingernails short and discourage scratching.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Treat itching:
		&lt;ul&gt;
			&lt;li&gt;Apply calamine lotion&lt;/li&gt;
			&lt;li&gt;In severe cases, give an oral antihistamine:Chlorphenamine 0.1 mg/kg/dose 6–8 hourly NB: Only children &gt;2 years.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Keep lesions clean and dry.
	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Acyclovir 20 mg/kg 4 times daily for 7 days.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Give oral Paracetamol for pain relief, continue to give every 6 hours (4 times / day) until pain gone&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Follow up in 7 days.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Refer if disseminated disease, involvement of the eye, pneumonia or features meningitis.&lt;/li&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Good personal and household hygiene to avoid spread of infection.&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Wash and soak sores in soapy water to soften and remove crusts.&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Apply antiseptic 8 hourly: Povidone iodine 5% cream or 10% ointment.&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Drain pus if fluctuant.&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Give antibiotic if extensive lesions: Cephalexin, oral, 12-25mg/kg/dose 6 hourly for 5 days&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Refer urgently if child has fever and or if infection extends to the muscles.&lt;/p&gt;</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">0..1</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/R4/codesystem-item-type.html#item-type-display">display</a></td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"/><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">Expressions: <ul><li style="font-size: 11px"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/uv/sdc/StructureDefinition/sdc-questionnaire-enableWhenExpression">Enable When</a>: <code>%resource.repeat(item).where(linkId='load-EmCare.C10.IT.DE33').answer.first().value=true</code></li></ul></td></tr>

	&lt;p&gt;➢Allow to heal spontaneously if few in number.
	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Apply a tincture of iodine BP to the core of individual lesions using an applicator.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Refer children with:
		&lt;ul&gt;
			&lt;li&gt;Extensive lesions&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;        &amp;#8211; No response to treatment&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;        &amp;#8211; Lesions close to the eye (to an ophthalmologist).&lt;/p&gt;</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">0..1</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/R4/codesystem-item-type.html#item-type-display">display</a></td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"/><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">Expressions: <ul><li style="font-size: 11px"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/uv/sdc/StructureDefinition/sdc-questionnaire-enableWhenExpression">Enable When</a>: <code>%resource.repeat(item).where(linkId='load-EmCare.C10.IT.DE34').answer.first().value=true</code></li></ul></td></tr>

	&lt;p&gt;➢May be left alone to wait for improvement&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Apply salicylic acid 15-20% to the warts
		&lt;ul&gt;
			&lt;li&gt;Protect surrounding skin with petroleum jelly&lt;/li&gt;
			&lt;li&gt;Apply daily to the wart and allow to dry&lt;/li&gt;
			&lt;li&gt;Occlude for 24 hours-Soften lesions by soaking in warm water, and remove loosened keratin.&lt;/li&gt;
			&lt;li&gt;Repeat process daily until the warts disappear.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Refer if extensive&lt;/p&gt;</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">0..1</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/R4/codesystem-item-type.html#item-type-display">display</a></td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"/><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">Expressions: <ul><li style="font-size: 11px"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/uv/sdc/StructureDefinition/sdc-questionnaire-enableWhenExpression">Enable When</a>: <code>%resource.repeat(item).where(linkId='load-EmCare.C10.IT.DE35').answer.first().value=true</code></li></ul></td></tr>

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;For scalp itching, scaling and dandruff: wash hair and scalp 2-3 times a week with selenium suphide 2.5% suspension.&lt;/li&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;

	&lt;/ul&gt;

		&lt;li&gt;&lt;b&gt;Give a first dose of intramuscular ampicillin. OR, if IM ampicillin is not avaialble, give a first dose of oral amoxicillin, at the dose indicated for Pneumonia&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Give fluids and breastmilk to treat diarrhoea at home (Plan A)&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Advise the mother when to return immediately&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Follow-up in 2 days if no improvement&lt;/p&gt;</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">0..1</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/R4/codesystem-item-type.html#item-type-display">display</a></td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"/><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">Expressions: <ul><li style="font-size: 11px"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/uv/sdc/StructureDefinition/sdc-questionnaire-enableWhenExpression">Enable When</a>: <code>%resource.repeat(item).where(linkId='load-EmCare.C10.IT.DE57').answer.first().value=true</code></li></ul></td></tr>
<tr style="border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px; vertical-align: top; background-color: #F7F7F7"><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px; white-space: nowrap; background-image: url(tbl_bck110.png)" id="item.EmCare.C10.IT.DE58" class="hierarchy"><img src="tbl_spacer.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vline.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vjoin.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="icon-q-display.png" alt="." style="background-color: #F7F7F7; background-color: inherit" title="Display" class="hierarchy"/> EmCare.C10.IT.DE58</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">&lt;h1&gt;Very Low Weight for Age&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;caps&quot;&gt;REFER&lt;/span&gt; to hospital for Kangaroo Mother Care&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;Treat to prevent low blood sugar&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

<tr style="border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px; vertical-align: top; background-color: white"><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px; white-space: nowrap; background-image: url(tbl_bck110.png)" id="item.EmCare.C10.IT.DE59" class="hierarchy"><img src="tbl_spacer.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vline.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vjoin.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="icon-q-display.png" alt="." style="background-color: white; background-color: inherit" title="Display" class="hierarchy"/> EmCare.C10.IT.DE59</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">&lt;h1&gt;No Feeding Problem&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Advise mother on giving home care to the young infant&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Praise the mother for feeding the infant well&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢If not breastfed, advise mother to continue feeding, and ensure good hygiene&lt;/p&gt;</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">0..1</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/R4/codesystem-item-type.html#item-type-display">display</a></td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"/><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: white; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">Expressions: <ul><li style="font-size: 11px"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/uv/sdc/StructureDefinition/sdc-questionnaire-enableWhenExpression">Enable When</a>: <code>%resource.repeat(item).where(linkId='load-EmCare.C10.IT.DE59').answer.first().value=true</code></li></ul></td></tr>
<tr style="border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px; vertical-align: top; background-color: #F7F7F7"><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px; white-space: nowrap; background-image: url(tbl_bck100.png)" id="item.EmCare.C10.IT.DE60" class="hierarchy"><img src="tbl_spacer.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vline.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="tbl_vjoin_end.png" alt="." style="background-color: inherit" class="hierarchy"/><img src="icon-q-display.png" alt="." style="background-color: #F7F7F7; background-color: inherit" title="Display" class="hierarchy"/> EmCare.C10.IT.DE60</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">&lt;h1&gt;Feeding Problem and / or Low Weight for Age&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Among infants who are breastfed:&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;If not well attached or not sucking effectively, teach correct positioning and attachment&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;If not able to attach well immediately, teach the mother to express breastmilk and feed from a cup&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;If breastfeeding less than 8 times in 24 hours, advise the mother to increase the frequency and to breastfeed as often and for as long as the infant wants, day and night&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;If the infant is receiving other foods or drinks, counsel the mother to increase breastfeeding, reduce other foods and drink and use a cup&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Among infants who are not breastfed: &lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Counsel about feeding&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Explain the guidelines for safe replacement feeding and correct preparation of breastmilk substitutes&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Identify concerns of mother and family about feeding&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;If mother is using a bottle, teach cup feeding&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Refer for breastfeeding counselling and possible relactation if the mother is alive and caring for the infant&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢If Low Weight for Age, advise the mother on how to feed and keep the low-weight infant warm at home&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢If the infant has thrush, teach the mother to treat thrush at home&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Give half-strength gentian violet (0.25%) 4 times daily for 7 days. Paint the mouth with gentian violet using a clean soft cloth wrapped around the finger. If gentian violet is not  avaialble, write a prescription for the medication for the mother and urge her to visit a pharmacy to purchase the medication.
 &lt;br /&gt;
➢Advise the mother on giving home care to the young infant&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Follow up Feeding Problem or Thrush in 2 days&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Among infants who are breastfed, follow up infants who have Low Weight for Age within 14 days&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Among infants who are not breastfed, follow up infants who have Low Weight for Age within 7 days&lt;/p&gt;</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">0..1</td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/R4/codesystem-item-type.html#item-type-display">display</a></td><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy"/><td style="vertical-align: top; text-align : left; background-color: #F7F7F7; border: 1px #F0F0F0 solid; padding:0px 4px 0px 4px" class="hierarchy">Expressions: <ul><li style="font-size: 11px"><a href="http://hl7.org/fhir/uv/sdc/StructureDefinition/sdc-questionnaire-enableWhenExpression">Enable When</a>: <code>%resource.repeat(item).where(linkId='load-EmCare.C10.IT.DE60').answer.first().value=true</code></li></ul></td></tr>

      <linkId value="EmCare.C10.IT.DE01"/>
      <text
            value="&lt;h1&gt;Very Severe Disease&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;Give one dose of rectal diazepam if convulsing now, repeat after 10 minutes if convulsion has not stopped&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;Give any pre-referral treatment immediately&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;Treat to prevent low blood sugar&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;Keep the child warm&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;Refer &lt;span class=&quot;caps&quot;&gt;URGENTLY&lt;/span&gt; to hospital*.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;*Exception: If lethargy is the only sign and child is dehydrated, rehydrated and assess.&lt;/p&gt;"/>
      <type value="display"/>
      <required value="false"/>
      <repeats value="false"/>
    </item>

      <linkId value="EmCare.C10.IT.DE02"/>
      <text
            value="&lt;h1&gt;Severe Pneumonia or Very Severe Disease&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;Give first dose of intramuscular Cefotaxime&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢If wheezing present, give one dose of rapid acting bronchodilator* pre-referral&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Treat the child to prevent low blood sugar&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Refer &lt;span class=&quot;caps&quot;&gt;URGENTLY&lt;/span&gt; to hospital&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;*Nebulized salbutamol, salbutamol inhaler with spacer, or subcutaneous epinephrine (adrenaline)&lt;/p&gt;"/>
      <type value="display"/>
      <required value="false"/>

      <linkId value="EmCare.C10.IT.DE03"/>
      <text
            value="&lt;h1&gt;Pneumonia&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢**Give oral Amoxicillin twice daily for 5 days**&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢If wheezing (or disappeared after inhaled salbutamol) give inhaled or oral salbutamol three times a day for 5 days*&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Soothe the throat and relieve the cough with a safe remedy.&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢If coughing for ≥14 days or recurrent wheeze, refer for possible TB or asthma assessment&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Advise mother when to return immediately&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Follow-up in 3 days&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Give oral Zinc once daily for 10-14 days.&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;*If inhaled bronchodilator is not available, oral salbutamol may be tried but not recommended for treatment of severe acute wheeze.&lt;/p&gt;"/>
      <type value="display"/>
      <required value="false"/>
      <repeats value="false"/>
    </item>

      <text
            value="&lt;h1&gt;Cough or Cold&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢If wheezing (or disappeared after inhaled salbutamol) give inhaled or oral salbutamol three times a day for 5 days**&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Soothe the throat and relieve the cough with a safe remedy.&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢If coughing for ≥14 days or recurrent wheeze, refer for possible TB or asthma assessment&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Advise mother when to return immediately&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Follow-up in 5 days if not improving&lt;/p&gt;"/>

      <text
            value="&lt;h1&gt;Severe Dehydration&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ If child has no other severe classification:* Give fluid for severe dehydration (plan C) OR&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;If child also has another severe classification:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

    * &lt;b&gt;Refer &lt;span class=&quot;caps&quot;&gt;URGENTLY&lt;/span&gt; to hospital with mother giving frequent sips of &lt;span class=&quot;caps&quot;&gt;ORS&lt;/span&gt; on the way.&lt;/b&gt;
    * &lt;b&gt;Advise the mother to continue breastfeeding.&lt;/b&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢If child is 2 years or older and there is cholera in your area, give oral co-trimoxazole twice daily for 3 days or oral erythromycin 4 times a day for 3 days for cholera.&lt;/p&gt;"/>

            value="&lt;h1&gt;Some Dehydration&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Give Plan B for some dehydration:&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Give &lt;span class=&quot;caps&quot;&gt;ORS&lt;/span&gt; over 4 hrs in clinic, reassess for dehydration and select appropriate plan to continue treatment&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;If mother must leave before completing treatment, give &lt;span class=&quot;caps&quot;&gt;ORS&lt;/span&gt; for 4 hr Plan B treatment plus 2 packets as recommended in Plan A&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;At home, give extra fluid (as much as the child will take)&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Give oral Zinc once daily for 10 &amp;#8211; 14 days&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Continue feeding (exclusive breastfeeding if under 6 months)&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢ &lt;b&gt;If child also has another severe classification:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;&lt;b&gt;Refer &lt;span class=&quot;caps&quot;&gt;URGENTLY&lt;/span&gt; to hospital with mother giving frequent sips of &lt;span class=&quot;caps&quot;&gt;ORS&lt;/span&gt; on the way.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;&lt;b&gt;Advise the mother to continue breastfeeding.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Advise mother when to return immediately.&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Follow-up in 5 days if not improving.&lt;/p&gt;"/>

            value="&lt;h1&gt;No Dehydration&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Give Plan A for no dehydration:&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Give extra fluid (as much as the child will take)&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Teach mother how to give &lt;span class=&quot;caps&quot;&gt;ORS&lt;/span&gt; and give 2 packets to use at home&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Give oral Zinc once daily for 14 days&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Continue feeding (exclusive breastfeeding if under 6 months)&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;

		&lt;li&gt;&lt;b&gt;Advise the mother to continue breastfeeding.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/li&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;

      <text
            value="&lt;h1&gt;Ringworm (tinea)&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Avoid sharing clothes, towels and toiletries (e.g. brushes and combs) to prevent spreading the infection to others.&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Wash and dry skin well before applying treatment.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Apply an imidazole (e.g. clotrimazole 1% cream) three times daily until two weeks after lesions have cleared.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;For scalp infections (tinea capitis) give oral fluconazole 6mg/kg once daily for 28 days&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;"/>

	&lt;p&gt;➢All close contacts should be treated simultaneously (even if not itchy).&lt;/p&gt;

		&lt;li&gt;Wash all bed linen and underwear in hot water&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Expose all bedding to direct sunlight.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Put on clean clothes after treatment.
 &lt;br /&gt;
➢Treat the child and contacts under 6 years of age with Permethrin:&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Apply permethrin 5% lotion. Leave on overnight and washoff in the morning (may be repeated after one week).&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Treatment may need to be repeated after one week.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Treat secondary bacterial infection, if present, with Oral Cephalexin 12-25mg/kg/dose 6 hourly for 5 days&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Treat contacts over 6 years of age with Benzyl Benzoate:&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Apply benzyl benzoate 25% from the neck to the toes. Allow the lotion to remain on the body for 24 hours, then wash off using soap and water&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Treatment may need to be repeated after one week.&lt;/li&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Limit contact with other children and pregnant women until all lesions have crusted.&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Ensure adequate hydration.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Cut fingernails short and discourage scratching.&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Treat itching:
		&lt;ul&gt;

		&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Keep lesions clean and dry.

      <linkId value="EmCare.C10.IT.DE60"/>
      <text
            value="&lt;h1&gt;Feeding Problem and / or Low Weight for Age&lt;/h1&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Among infants who are breastfed:&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;If not well attached or not sucking effectively, teach correct positioning and attachment&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;If not able to attach well immediately, teach the mother to express breastmilk and feed from a cup&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;If breastfeeding less than 8 times in 24 hours, advise the mother to increase the frequency and to breastfeed as often and for as long as the infant wants, day and night&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;If the infant is receiving other foods or drinks, counsel the mother to increase breastfeeding, reduce other foods and drink and use a cup&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Among infants who are not breastfed: &lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Counsel about feeding&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Explain the guidelines for safe replacement feeding and correct preparation of breastmilk substitutes&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Identify concerns of mother and family about feeding&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;If mother is using a bottle, teach cup feeding&lt;/li&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Refer for breastfeeding counselling and possible relactation if the mother is alive and caring for the infant&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢If Low Weight for Age, advise the mother on how to feed and keep the low-weight infant warm at home&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢If the infant has thrush, teach the mother to treat thrush at home&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;ul&gt;
		&lt;li&gt;Give half-strength gentian violet (0.25%) 4 times daily for 7 days. Paint the mouth with gentian violet using a clean soft cloth wrapped around the finger. If gentian violet is not  avaialble, write a prescription for the medication for the mother and urge her to visit a pharmacy to purchase the medication.
 &lt;br /&gt;
➢Advise the mother on giving home care to the young infant&lt;/li&gt;
	&lt;/ul&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Follow up Feeding Problem or Thrush in 2 days&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Among infants who are breastfed, follow up infants who have Low Weight for Age within 14 days&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;p&gt;➢Among infants who are not breastfed, follow up infants who have Low Weight for Age within 7 days&lt;/p&gt;"/>
      <type value="display"/>
      <required value="false"/>
      <repeats value="false"/>
    </item>
